

CREATE DATABASE TecMIS_DB;

//////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
CREATE TABLE User (
    Username VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    First_Name VARCHAR(50),
    Last_Name VARCHAR(50),
    Designation VARCHAR(50),
    Phone_Number VARCHAR(15),
    Email VARCHAR(100),
    Password VARCHAR(255),
    PRIMARY KEY (Username)
);

ALTER TABLE User
ADD Profile_Pic_Path VARCHAR(255);


//////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

CREATE TABLE Admin (
    Admin_Username VARCHAR(50) PRIMARY KEY
);

////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////


CREATE TABLE Lecturer (
    Lecturer_Username VARCHAR(50) PRIMARY KEY
);

/////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

CREATE TABLE Technical_officer (
    TO_Username VARCHAR(50) PRIMARY KEY
);

////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
CREATE TABLE Timetable (
    Timetable_id CHAR(10),
    Admin_Username VARCHAR(50),
    Content LONGTEXT,
    PRIMARY KEY (Timetable_id)
);
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
CREATE TABLE Student (
    Student_Username VARCHAR(50),
    Timetable_id CHAR(10),
    PRIMARY KEY (Student_Username)
);

/////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

CREATE TABLE Course_unit (
    Course_code CHAR(10),
    Course_Name VARCHAR(100),
    Course_type VARCHAR(20),
    Theory_hours INT,
    Practical_hours INT,
    Credits INT,
    Lecturer_Username VARCHAR(50),
    Admin_Username VARCHAR(50),
    PRIMARY KEY (Course_code)
);

//////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
CREATE TABLE Student_course_unit (
    Student_Username VARCHAR(50),
    Course_code CHAR(10),
    PRIMARY KEY (Student_Username, Course_code)
);

////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

CREATE TABLE Medical (
    Medical_id CHAR(10),
    Submission_date VARCHAR(15),
    Status VARCHAR(15),
    Start_date VARCHAR(15),
    End_date VARCHAR(15),
    Reason VARCHAR(100),
    Course_code CHAR(10),
    Student_Username VARCHAR(50),
    TO_Username VARCHAR(50),
    PRIMARY KEY (Medical_id)
);

/////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

CREATE TABLE Attendance (
    Course_code CHAR(10),
    Student_Username VARCHAR(50),
    Session_Type VARCHAR(15),
    Session_date VARCHAR(50),
    Status VARCHAR(15),
    TO_Username VARCHAR(50),
    Medical_id CHAR(10),
    PRIMARY KEY (Student_Username, Course_code, Session_Type, Session_date)
);

///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

CREATE TABLE Lecturer_Attendance (
    Lecturer_Username VARCHAR(50),
    Student_Username VARCHAR(50),
    Course_code CHAR(10),
    PRIMARY KEY (Lecturer_Username, Student_Username, Course_code)
);

/////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

CREATE TABLE Marks (
    Student_Username VARCHAR(50),
    Lecturer_Username VARCHAR(50),
    Course_code CHAR(10),
    Medical_id CHAR(10),
    Quiz1 FLOAT,
    Quiz2 FLOAT,
    Quiz3 FLOAT,
    Quiz4 FLOAT,
    Assessment_01 FLOAT,
    Assessment_02 FLOAT,
    Mid_Practical FLOAT,
    Mid_Theory FLOAT,
    End_Practical FLOAT,
    End_Theory FLOAT,
    PRIMARY KEY (Student_Username, Course_code)
);

//////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

CREATE TABLE Lecturer_Medical (
    Lecturer_Username VARCHAR(50),
    Medical_id CHAR(10),
    PRIMARY KEY (Lecturer_Username, Medical_id)
);

//////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

CREATE TABLE Timetable_TO_Officer (
    Timetable_id CHAR(10),
    TO_Username VARCHAR(50),
    PRIMARY KEY (Timetable_id, TO_Username)
);

////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

CREATE TABLE Notice (
    Notice_id CHAR(10),
    Title VARCHAR(50),
    Publish_date DATE,
    Admin_Username VARCHAR(50),
    PRIMARY KEY (Notice_id)
);

/////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

CREATE TABLE Notice_Lecturer (
    Notice_id CHAR(10),
    Lecturer_Username VARCHAR(50),
    PRIMARY KEY (Notice_id, Lecturer_Username)
);

/////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

CREATE TABLE Notice_Student (
    Notice_id CHAR(10),
    Student_Username VARCHAR(50),
    PRIMARY KEY (Notice_id, Student_Username)
);

//////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

CREATE TABLE Notice_TO_Officer (
    Notice_id CHAR(10),
    TO_Username VARCHAR(50),
    PRIMARY KEY (Notice_id, TO_Username)
);







///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
ALTER TABLE Admin
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Admin_Username) REFERENCES User(Username);

////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

ALTER TABLE Lecturer
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Lecturer_Username) REFERENCES User(Username);

///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

ALTER TABLE Technical_officer
ADD FOREIGN KEY (TO_Username) REFERENCES User(Username);

//////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////


ALTER TABLE Timetable
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Admin_Username) REFERENCES Admin(Admin_Username);

///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

ALTER TABLE Student
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Student_Username) REFERENCES User(Username);

ALTER TABLE Student
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Timetable_id) REFERENCES Timetable(Timetable_id);

////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

ALTER TABLE Course_unit
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Lecturer_Username) REFERENCES Lecturer(Lecturer_Username);

ALTER TABLE Course_unit
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Admin_Username) REFERENCES Admin(Admin_Username);

/////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
ALTER TABLE Student_course_unit
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Student_Username) REFERENCES Student(Student_Username);

ALTER TABLE Student_course_unit
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Course_code) REFERENCES Course_unit(Course_code);

///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////


ALTER TABLE Medical
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Student_Username) REFERENCES Student(Student_Username);

ALTER TABLE Medical
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Course_code) REFERENCES Course_unit(Course_code);

ALTER TABLE Medical
ADD FOREIGN KEY (TO_Username) REFERENCES Technical_officer(TO_Username);

//////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

ALTER TABLE Attendance
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Student_Username) REFERENCES Student(Student_Username);

ALTER TABLE Attendance
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Course_code) REFERENCES Course_unit(Course_code);

ALTER TABLE Attendance
ADD FOREIGN KEY (TO_Username) REFERENCES Technical_officer(TO_Username);

ALTER TABLE Attendance
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Medical_id) REFERENCES Medical(Medical_id);

////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

ALTER TABLE Lecturer_Attendance
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Lecturer_Username) REFERENCES Lecturer(Lecturer_Username);

ALTER TABLE Lecturer_Attendance
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Student_Username) REFERENCES Student(Student_Username);

ALTER TABLE Lecturer_Attendance
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Course_code) REFERENCES Course_unit(Course_code);

////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

ALTER TABLE Marks
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Student_Username) REFERENCES Student(Student_Username);

ALTER TABLE Marks
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Lecturer_Username) REFERENCES Lecturer(Lecturer_Username);

ALTER TABLE Marks
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Course_code) REFERENCES Course_unit(Course_code);

ALTER TABLE Marks
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Medical_id) REFERENCES Medical(Medical_id);

//////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////



ALTER TABLE Lecturer_Medical
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Lecturer_Username) REFERENCES Lecturer(Lecturer_Username);

ALTER TABLE Lecturer_Medical
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Medical_id) REFERENCES Medical(Medical_id);

///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

ALTER TABLE Timetable_TO_Officer
ADD FOREIGN KEY (TO_Username) REFERENCES Technical_officer(TO_Username);

ALTER TABLE Timetable_TO_Officer
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Timetable_id) REFERENCES Timetable(Timetable_id);

////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////


ALTER TABLE Notice
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Admin_Username) REFERENCES Admin(Admin_Username);

////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////


ALTER TABLE Notice_Lecturer
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Notice_id) REFERENCES Notice(Notice_id);

ALTER TABLE Notice_Lecturer
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Lecturer_Username) REFERENCES Lecturer(Lecturer_Username);

///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

ALTER TABLE Notice_Student
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Notice_id) REFERENCES Notice(Notice_id);

ALTER TABLE Notice_Student
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Student_Username) REFERENCES Student(Student_Username);

/////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////



ALTER TABLE Notice_TO_Officer
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Notice_id) REFERENCES Notice(Notice_id);

ALTER TABLE Notice_TO_Officer
ADD FOREIGN KEY (TO_Username) REFERENCES Technical_officer(TO_Username);

////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

CREATE TABLE LectureMaterials (

Material_ID INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
Course_Code VARCHAR(10),
Title VARCHAR(255),
Description TEXT,
File_Path VARCHAR(500),
Uploaded_Date TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

/////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

CREATE TABLE newtimetable (
    course_code VARCHAR(20) PRIMARY KEY,
    course_name VARCHAR(100),
    start_time VARCHAR(20),
    end_time VARCHAR(20),
    date VARCHAR(20)
);
